## Support Tier Legend

| Tier | Meaning |
|------|---------|
| 1 | **Tier 1** — Automated trace tests + recent HIL validation |
| 2 | **Tier 2** — Automated tests (no HIL) + community confirmation |
| 3 | **Tier 3** — Compiles / best-effort — no guarantees |
